Why is cut_oxydized_copper_slabs funny? my friend keeps asking me

I'm not sure why cut_oxydized_copper_slabs is funny, but I guess it has something to do with the word "copper" sounding like a swear word.

My friend thinks it's funny because it's a play on words. When you cut copper, it becomes oxidized. So the phrase "cut_oxydized_copper_slabs" is basically saying "cut the F-ing copper!"
